nofollow" target="_blank">https://securingtomorrow.mcafee.com/mcafee-labs/dropping-files-temp-folder-raises-security-concerns/</a></p><p id="32ad" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mm mn hd mo b mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj gw bl">Many attackers use it in the wild because it’ very easy to use and it’ supported by the office software with RTF files.</p><p id="6b70" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mm mn hd mo b mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj gw bl">So, in our case, a file named 8.t is dropped on %TMP% folder.</p><p id="9dfc" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mm mn hd mo b mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj gw bl">So now, we have to debug the malicious document to find how the file 8.t is used and find this runPE.</p><h2 id="feb3" class="oj ok hd bg ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz pa pb pc pd pe pf pg bl">Debugging of the shellcode</h2><p id="6872" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mm mn hd mo b mp ph mr ms mt pi mv mw mx pj mz na nb pk nd ne nf pl nh ni nj gw bl">At the start of the analysis, we think the process EQNEDT32.exe is created by Winword.exe using the function CreateProcess. So we decided to set a breakpoint at the call of his function.</p><p id="3da9" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mm mn hd mo b mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj gw bl">But EQNEDT32.exe is invoked by Winword.exe using COM Object. It’s not CreateProcess that used and Winword.exe is not the parent process of EQNEDT32.exe. So we have to attach the debugger when EQNEDT32.exe is launched.</p><p id="a7dd" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mm mn hd mo b mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj gw bl">For that, we used a technique named Image File Execution Options that was documented by Microsoft. <a class="ah px" href="https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/mithuns/2010/03/24/image-file-execution-options-ifeo/" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank">https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/mithuns/2010/03/24/image-file-execution-options-ifeo/</a></p><p id="121e" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mm mn hd mo b mp mq mr ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz
